Revised October 27, 2016
Please Help Us Keep Listings Current
IMS updates the telephone directory on a weekly schedule. To make changes or additions, click
here or submit a ServiceNow incident.
***Please note that we are not given a list of new employees or employees that change
departments, you must submit the requests for these changes.***
If you would like to print a copy of the telephone directory, click here.

TELEPHONE REFERENCE GUIDE
TELEPHONE PROBLEMS
If you have ANY problems with your telephones, need telephones moved, need additional features, or would like training, please
call the Telephone Administration Section at 535-7272.

LONG DISTANCE
Remember there is a cost for all long distance calls and that department heads review the calls made by their employees. Long
distance calls are billed back to each department.

LONG DISTANCE with a Telephone Access Card
For LONG DISTANCE
Dial
"9" then "1", then the area code and number.
Listen for a "Fast Busy" tone.
Enter Your Access Code from the front of your Telephone Access Card.
Press "B" (the 2 button) for Business calls or
"P" (the 7 button) for Personal calls.
Example: If your access code is "98765"
Business: 9 1 801 123 4567----98765 2
Personal: 9 1 801 123 4567----98765 7

LONG DISTANCE without a Telephone Access Card
For "IN STATE" LONG DISTANCE dial "9", dial "1", dial "801" or “435”, and then the normal 7 digit number.
For "OUT OF STATE" LONG DISTANCE dial "9", dial "1", area code, and the normal 7 digit number.

DIRECTORY ASSISTANCE
Since U.S. West now charges for directory assistance, it is important to use directory assistance only when it is necessary, i.e., the
number is not in the telephone book, business card, etc. Directory assistance is billed back to each department.
For directory assistance to any location within the State of Utah, dial 9-1-555-1212.
For directory assistance within the city, dial 9-1411.
For any location outside the State of Utah, dial 9-1 (Area Code of location in question) and 555-1212.

Page 123 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

OPERATOR ASSISTANCE
To reach a U.S. West operator, dial 9-0.
To reach a long distance operator, dial 9-0-0 (the second 0 should work at your home as well).

Page 124 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

INSTRUCTIONS FOR ELECTRONIC (MULTIPLE BUTTON)
TELEPHONES

CALL FORWARD
Allows you to program your telephone so calls to your extension will ring at another number. This feature is used when you do not
want to be interrupted or you are away from your desk. Some telephones have automatic call forward which forwards the calls if the
telephone is busy or is not answered within 3 rings.

HOW TO USE
Without lifting hand set:
1. Press Call Forward key (light will flash).
2. Dial number where call is to be forwarded.
3. Press Call Forward key again (light will be steady, indicating that all calls
have been forwarded).
NOTE: The person that you have your calls forwarded to can call you and give you your messages.
To cancel Call Forward, simply press the Call Forward key and the light will go out.

CALL TRANSFER
Allows you to transfer a call to another number. This feature is used when someone has reached you by mistake or they wish to talk
to another person after they have talked to you.

HOW TO USE
With user on the same line:
1. Press Call Transfer key
2. Dial number
3. Announce the caller
4. Press Call Transfer key again
5. Hang up
A COMMON PROBLEM IS FORGETTING TO PRESS THE TRANSFER KEY THE SECOND TIME.

CONFERENCE
Allows you to bring additional people into your conversation.

HOW TO USE
1. Receive or place a call
2. Press Conference key
3. Dial the number
4. Announce to the person you are calling that you would like to setup a conference call.

Page 125 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

5. Press Conference key again and all parties will be connected.
You can repeat this procedure up to 6 times.

CALL PICK UP
This feature is used when there are several telephones in one room and a person would like to answer someone else's telephone. The
telephone needs to be programmed to tell them which other phones they are allowed to answer. Please call 535-7272 for further
information.
NOTE: There is no light beside the Call Pick Up key.

RING AGAIN
This feature is used when you try to call someone and get a busy signal. This feature tells the system to monitor the status of their
phone; and as soon as they hang up, it will ring your telephone. This feature can ONLY be used for telephones connected to the same
PBX.

HOW TO USE
When you get a busy signal:
1. Press Ring Again key. (A steady light will come on).
2. Hang up
To respond:
1. Set will buzz (Ring Again light will flash). If you are busy, you may ignore this (no harm done).
2. Lift hand set
3. Press Ring Again key (the number will automatically be dialed for you).
To cancel (without lifting hand set):
1. Press Ring Again key (light will go out).

DIAL INTERCOM
Allows an electronic telephone to make a voice announcement to another electronic telephone. A typical use would be for a
receptionist to "page" another individual. The receptionist's message will be heard through the speaker (not the hand set). The
person that is called will hear the message without picking up their handset, but you must lift the handset to talk. If the number dialed
is busy, the intercom light will come on and a brief ring will be heard. This is a special feature and not all electronic telephones have
it.

HOW TO USE
To call someone on the intercom:
1. Press the Intercom key
2. Dial the special 2-digit intercom number
3. Give message
4. If the called party is on the line, the person calling will hear a continuation of ringing.
5. If the calling party wants two-way communications, they can pick up their hand set.

SPEED CALL
Used to call frequently called numbers by dialing 1 or 2 digits. This feature is limited to electronic phones that are
equipped with a Speed Call button (please call 535-7272 for further information). The standard speed call
capacity will allow for up to 10 numbers (8 digits long).

Page 126 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

HOW TO USE
Lift hand set:
1. Press Speed Call key
2. Dial 1 or 2-digit speed code
3. Number is automatically dialed
To program:
1. Do not lift hand set
2. Press Speed Call key
3. Dial the 1 or 2-digit number you wish to use for speed code.
4. Key in telephone number
5. Press Speed Call key again

CALL PARK
To be used in conjunction with a paging system. This feature eliminates the need for a paged person to call the
receptionist to have a call connected to their set. Instead, the receptionist who is giving the page can indicate a
special number where the call is "parked"; then the paged person can go to any telephone, dial in that special
parked number and the call will be automatically connected.
HOW TO USE
Using Park Key to Park Call:
With user on same line
1. Press the Park key
2. Dial number where call is to be parked (usually the person's normal office phone number).
3. Press Park key.
To retrieve:
1. Press Park key
2. Dial parked number (usually the person's normal office phone
number).
3. Call is automatically connected
Using Transfer Key to Park Calls:
With user on the same line:
1. Press Call Transfer key or Conference key
2. Dial 171
3. Dial number where call is to be "parked"
4. Press Call Transfer key or Conference key again
To retrieve:
1. Lift handset
2. Dial 172
3. Dial number on which call is "parked"
4. Call is automatically connected

INSTRUCTIONS FOR STANDARD (SINGLE BUTTON) TELEPHONES

Page 127 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

PERMANENT HOLD
Allows you to put your call on hold. This eliminates the need for putting your hand over the hand set if you wanted to talk
privately with someone at your desk.

HOW TO USE
1. Press the switch hook quickly (one of the two buttons in the handset cradle).
2. Dial #4
3. Hang up
To retrieve:
1. Lift hand set

CONSULTATION HOLD
Allows you to put your call on hold and then call another number. The person on hold cannot hear the conversation that you
have with the second party. Therefore, it is different than Call Transfer or a Conference Call.

HOW TO USE
1. Press the switch hook quickly (one of the two buttons in the handset cradle).
2. Dial the number of the party that you want to consult with.
3. Consult privately
4. Consulting party hangs up
5. You are automatically reconnected to your original call.

CALL FORWARD
Allows you to program your telephone so calls to your extension will ring at another number. This feature is used when you
do not want to be interrupted, or you will be away from your desk. Some telephones will have automatic call forward in
which calls will be forwarded if the telephone is busy or is not answered within 3 rings.
A COMMON PROBLEM IS CONFUSION BETWEEN CALL FORWARD, THE AUTOMATIC CALL FORWARD
AND CALL TRANSFER. THEY ARE DIFFERENT.

Page 128 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

HOW TO USE
Lift hand set:
1. Dial No. 1
2. Dial number where call is to be forwarded
3. Hang up
To cancel:
1. Dial #1
NOTE: The person that you have your calls forwarded to can call you and give you your messages.

CALL TRANSFER
Allows you to transfer a call to another number. This feature is used when someone has reached you by mistake or they wish to
talk to another person after they have talked to you.

HOW TO USE
1. Press the switch hook quickly (one of the two buttons in the handset cradle).
2. Dial the number
3. Announce the caller
4. Hang up

CONFERENCE
Allows you to bring additional people into your conversation.

HOW TO USE
1. Press the switch hook quickly (one of the two buttons in the handset cradle).
2. Dial the number
3. Announce to the person you are calling that you would like to setup a conference call.
4. Flash with the switch hook.5. All parties are now connected.
You can repeat this feature up to 6 times.

CALL PICK UP
This feature is used where there are several telephones in one room and a person would like to answer someone else's telephone. The
telephones need to be programmed to tell them which other phones they are allowed to answer. Programming can be done by the
Telephone Administration Section.

HOW TO USE
1. Lift your handset
2. Dial 13
3. Answer the call as you normally would.

RING AGAIN
This is a very handy feature to be used when you try to call someone and get a busy signal. This feature tells the system to monitor
the status of their phone; and as soon as they hang up, your telephone will ring. This feature can ONLY be used for telephones at the
same PBX.

Page 129 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

HOW TO USE
If you get a busy signal:
1. Quickly press the switch hook (one of the two buttons in the handset cradle).
2. Dial 11
3. Hang up
When the other party hangs up:
1. You will hear a short burst of rings
2. Lift handset during ringing
3. Call is automatically connected
To cancel, lift hand set:
1. Dial 12
2. Hang up

CALL PARK
To be used in conjunction with a paging system. This feature eliminates the need for a paged person to call the receptionist to have
a call connected to their set. instead, the receptionist, while giving the page, can indicate that the call is "parked". The paged person
can then go to any telephone and receive the call.

HOW TO USE
To park a call:
1. Lift hand set
2. Quickly press the switch hook (one of the tow buttons in the handset cradle).
3. Dial 171
4. Dial number where you wish to park the call (use the telephone number of the person being called).
5. Hang up.
To retrieve the call:
1. Lift hand set
2. Dial 172
3. Dial the number on which the call is parked (should be your City telephone number).
4. The call is automatically connected.

Voice Mail
Voice Mail Setup
1.

From your main telephone line, dial 6288. Or 535-6288 Your personal voice mail is setup on your extension.

2.

When the system answers, it prompts you for your mail box number and then for a temporary password, enter (on the dial pad
of your telephone) 72+ your extension.

3.

Change your password, press 4 to go to personal options, 2 to go to administrative options, 1 to go to the password
menu. Press 5 to change
your personal password and then follow the directions from the system.

4.

Change your greeting, press 4 to go to personal options, 3 to go to the greetings menu. The system will instruct you how

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

to change your name and greetings.
5.

For help and more information call IMS Customer Support at Ext. 7272.

Customizing Your Mailbox
1.

Enter your mailbox by dialing 6288, or 535-6288 then enter your password. (You are now in the main menu ) At any point in
the menus, you can backup by dialing *.

2.

Change your password, press 4 to go to personal options, 2 to go to administrative options, 1 to go to the password
menu. Press 5 to change your personal password and then follow the directions from the system.

3.

Change your greeting, press 4 to go to personal options, 2 to go to administrative options, 3 to go to the greetings menu.
The system will instruct you how to change your name and greetings.

4.

Date and time playback, press 4 to go to the personal options, 2 to go to administrative options, 4 to turn on or off the date
and time playback.

5.

To set up the schedule for pager notification, press 4 to go to personal options, 4 to go to the notification schedule. The
voice prompts will now instruct you on how to set up your pager notification schedule.

Using Voice Mail
1.

To check for mail messages, dial 6288 (from within the city system), or 535-6288 (from outside the city system).

2.

When the voice mail system answers, dial # then your mailbox number.

3.

Enter your password.

4.

Dial 1 to listen to your messages. To skip a message, dial #.

5.

To fast forward within a message, dial 3. To back up, dial 1.

6.

After listening to the message, you can delete it by dialing 7, or you can save

7.

To exit the voice mail system, press * until it says good bye.

ORDERING VOICE MAIL
If you would like to have voice mail, please call Customer Service at 535-7272. There is a one time installation charge of $12.00 and
a monthly fee of $8.00.
When using the voice mail system, your telephone extension is your mail box number. In some special cases alternate numbers have
been assigned.

HOW TO SEND A MESSAGE TO OTHER VOICE MAIL USERS
After entering the system at the Main Menu:
1. Press 2 to record the message.
2. Press # when finished recording.
3. Press 1 to replay your message (optional).
4. Press * to re-record if you were not satisfied with first message.
5. Enter the destination mailbox number or press # to spell the name.
6. Press 0 to select message delivery options (Private, Urgent, Message Confirmation, Future Delivery).
7. Press # to send the message.
8. Press * for no more destinations.

HOW TO RETRIEVE YOUR MESSAGES
When calling from outside the city telephone system:
1. Call you own telephone number
2. When you hear your greeting press 5
3. Enter your password
4. Now you are at the Main Menu.

GENERAL TIPS
Page 132 Revised: 10/28/2016

SALT LAKE CITY CORPORATION PHONE DIRECTORY

A few general tips that will help you as you use the system:
0 = HELP
Ø Press 0 if you need help, more explanation, or want more options. (If you don't press anything, the system will repeat the
previous options to help you.) Press 0-0 while in your mailbox to reach an attendant if one is available.
* = CANCEL or EXIT from a menu
Ø Press * any time you want to cancel a previous entry or exit from a menu. When you exit from a menu, you "back up" to a
previous menu. For instance, * in the Administrative Options menu takes you back to the Personal Options menu; one more *
returns you to the Main Menu where you can start all over again! Pressing * while at the Main Menu disconnects you from the
system.
# = SKIP or BYPASS
Ø Press # to bypass a subscriber's personal greeting with the exception on an extended absence greeting.
Ø New subscribers begin using the system with Standard Prompts which prompt for only Review and Send at the Main Menu.
Check Receipt and Personal Options are available to you, but you will not be prompted for them. As soon as you are
comfortable with the basics, you will probably want to use Extended Prompts to hear prompts for all options. Rapid prompt can
be used when you are very comfortable with the systems available options. If you have a Guest call IMS Customer Support at
535-7272.
Ø REMEMBER that when a message has been erased, you cannot get it back.
Ø Saved messages are "archived" for only 30 days at which time you will be given the opportunity to resave or delete the
messages.
Ø Playback Controls can be used by keying numbers:
Rewind 10 seconds 1
Rewind to the beginning 1-1
Pause or resume playback 2
Fast-forwards 10 seconds 3
Forward to the end 3-3
Play message slower 4
For envelope information 5
Play message faster 6
Increase the volume 8 normal, 9 louder
Ø A maximum of 25 messages can be saved.
Ø Unheard messages are saved for 15 days.
Ø The maximum length for a message left by a caller is 10 minutes.
